### Music Theory and Music Math

- `C.1`
  Equation:

  \[m_{\mathrm{C_1}}^+ = M_{\mathrm{C_1}}m_{\mathrm{C_1}}^-, \qquad \tau_{\mathrm{C_1}} = \|L m_{\mathrm{C_1}}^+\|_2\]

  Variable legend: `m in R^12` is the pitch-tension vector; `tau` is post-line tension.
  Reading: fluid carriage line.
  Confidence: mixed

### Compression

- `C.1`

  \[g_{\mathrm{C_1}}^+ = \mathrm{Coll}\!\left(\Phi_{\mathrm{C_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}}(\mathrm{Expand}(g_{\mathrm{C_1}}^-))\right)\]

  Variable legend: `g` is the replay seed and `rho` the expanded state.
  Reading: fluid carriage line.
  Confidence: mixed

### Hacking Theory

- `C.1`
  Equation:

  \[\pi_{\mathrm{C_1}}^+ = \pi_{\mathrm{C_1}}^- \oplus e_{\mathrm{C_1}}, \qquad e_{\mathrm{C_1}} \in E_{\mathrm{safe}} \iff \mathrm{seal}(e_{\mathrm{C_1}})=1 \land \mathrm{budget}(e_{\mathrm{C_1}})\le B_{\mathrm{C_1}}\]

  Variable legend: `pi` is the route, `e_line` the next admissible edge, `B_line` the seal budget.
  Reading: fluid carriage line.
  Confidence: mixed

### Game Theory

- `C.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{C_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{C_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{C_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{C_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
